stderr | src/lib/spClient.spec.ts > ensureConfig > throws when placeholders remain
ensureConfig typeof function source function ensureConfig(envOverride) {
  const overrideRecord = envOverride;
  const hasExplicitOverride = envOverride !== void 0;
  const _pickSite = () => {
    const primary = (0,__vite_ssr_import_0__.readEnv)("VITE_SP_SITE_RELATIVE", "", overrideRecord).trim();
    if (primary) return primary;
    const legacy = (0,__vite_ssr_import_0__.readEnv)("VITE_SP_SITE", "", overrideRecord).trim();
    return legacy;
  };
  const isPlaceholder = (s) => {
    const normalized = (s ?? "").trim();
    if (!normalized) return true;
    const lower = normalized.toLowerCase();
    if (normalized.includes("<") || normalized.includes("__")) return true;
    if (/<[^>]+>/.test(normalized)) return true;
    if (lower.includes("fill") || lower.includes("your")) return true;
    return false;
  };
  const validateAndNormalize = (resourceRaw, siteRaw) => {
    const overrideResource = sanitizeEnvValue(resourceRaw);
    const overrideSiteRel = sanitizeEnvValue(siteRaw);
    if (isPlaceholder(overrideResource) || isPlaceholder(overrideSiteRel)) {
      throw new Error([
        "SharePoint 謗･邯夊ｨｭ螳壹′譛ｪ螳御ｺ・〒縺吶・,
        "VITE_SP_RESOURCE 萓・ https://contoso.sharepoint.com・域忰蟆ｾ繧ｹ繝ｩ繝・す繝･荳崎ｦ・ｼ・,
        "VITE_SP_SITE_RELATIVE 萓・ /sites/AuditSystem・亥・鬆ｭ繧ｹ繝ｩ繝・す繝･蠢・医・譛ｫ蟆ｾ荳崎ｦ・ｼ・,
        "`.env` 繧貞ｮ溷､縺ｧ譖ｴ譁ｰ縺励・幕逋ｺ繧ｵ繝ｼ繝舌・繧貞・襍ｷ蜍輔＠縺ｦ縺上□縺輔＞縲・
      ].join("\n"));
    };
    let overrideUrl;
    try {
      overrideUrl = new URL(overrideResource);
    } catch {
      throw new Error(`VITE_SP_RESOURCE 縺ｮ蠖｢蠑上′荳肴ｭ｣縺ｧ縺・ ${overrideResource}`);
    };
    if (overrideUrl.protocol !== "https:" || !/\.sharepoint\.com$/i.test(overrideUrl.hostname)) {
      throw new Error(`VITE_SP_RESOURCE 縺ｮ蠖｢蠑上′荳肴ｭ｣縺ｧ縺・ ${overrideResource}`);
    };
    const siteCandidate = normalizeSiteRelative(overrideSiteRel);
    if (!siteCandidate.startsWith("/sites/") && !siteCandidate.startsWith("/teams/")) {
      throw new Error(`VITE_SP_SITE_RELATIVE 縺ｮ蠖｢蠑上′荳肴ｭ｣縺ｧ縺・ ${overrideSiteRel}`);
    };
    const resource = normalizeResource(overrideUrl.origin);
    const siteRel = siteCandidate;
    return { resource, siteRel, baseUrl: `${resource}${siteRel}/_api/web` };
  };
  if (hasExplicitOverride) {
    return validateAndNormalize(
      envOverride?.VITE_SP_RESOURCE ?? "",
      envOverride?.VITE_SP_SITE_RELATIVE ?? envOverride?.VITE_SP_SITE ?? ""
    );
  };
  if (shouldBypassSharePointConfig(overrideRecord)) {
    return { resource: "", siteRel: "", baseUrl: "" };
  };
  const baseConfig = (0,__vite_ssr_import_0__.getAppConfig)();
  const config = envOverride ? { ...baseConfig, ...envOverride } : baseConfig;
  if (config.VITE_E2E) {
    const resource = FALLBACK_SP_RESOURCE;
    const siteRel = FALLBACK_SP_SITE_RELATIVE;
    return { resource, siteRel, baseUrl: `${resource}${siteRel}/_api/web` };
  };
  const rawResource = sanitizeEnvValue(config.VITE_SP_RESOURCE ?? "");
  const rawSiteRel = sanitizeEnvValue(
    config.VITE_SP_SITE_RELATIVE ?? config.VITE_SP_SITE ?? ""
  );
  return validateAndNormalize(rawResource, rawSiteRel);
}
